                                 'title': title,
                                 'author': author,
                                 'isbn': isbn,
                                 'genre': genre,
                                 'publisher': publisher,
                                 'year': int(year),
                                 'description': description,
                                 'status': status,
                                 'avg_rating': float(avg_rating)
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading books data: {e}")
             return books
         
         
         def write_books(books: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(books_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in books:
                         f.write(f"{b['book_id']}|{b['title']}|{b['author']}|{b['isbn']}|{b['genre']}|{b['publisher']}|{b['year']}|{b['description']}|{b['status']}|{b['avg_rating']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing books data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_borrowings() -> List[Dict]:
             borrowings = []
             try:
                 with open(borrowings_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         borrow_id, username, book_id, borrow_date, due_date, return_date, status, fine_amount = parts
                         try:
                             borrowings.append({
                                 'borrow_id': int(borrow_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                                 'due_date': due_date,
                                 'return_date': return_date if return_date else None,
                                 'status': status,
                                 'fine_amount': float(fine_amount)
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading borrowings data: {e}")
             return borrowings
         
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(borrowings_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in borrowings:
                         return_date = b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                         f.write(f"{b['borrow_id']}|{b['username']}|{b['book_id']}|{b['borrow_date']}|{b['due_date']}|{return_date}|{b['status']}|{b['fine_amount']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing borrowings data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_reservations() -> List[Dict]:
             reservations = []
             try:
                 with open(reservations_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         reservation_id, username, book_id, reservation_date, status = parts
                         try:
                             reservations.append({
                                 'reservation_id': int(reservation_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'reservation_date': reservation_date,
                                 'status': status
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading reservations data: {e}")
             return reservations
         
         
         def write_reservations(reservations: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(reservations_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reservations:
                         f.write(f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['reservation_date']}|{r['status']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing reservations data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_reviews() -> List[Dict]:
             reviews = []
             try:
                 with open(reviews_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         review_id, username, book_id, rating, review_text, review_date = parts
                         try:
                             reviews.append({
                                 'review_id': int(review_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'rating': int(rating),
                                 'review_text': review_text,
                                 'review_date': review_date
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading reviews data: {e}")
             return reviews
         
         
         def write_reviews(reviews: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(reviews_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reviews:
                         f.write(f"{r['review_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing reviews data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_fines() -> List[Dict]:
             fines = []
             try:
                 with open(fines_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         fine_id, username, borrow_id, amount, status, date_issued = parts
                         try:
                             fines.append({
                                 'fine_id': int(fine_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'borrow_id': int(borrow_id),
                                 'amount': float(amount),
                                 'status': status,
                                 'date_issued': date_issued
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading fines data: {e}")
             return fines
         
         
         def write_fines(fines: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(fines_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for fn in fines:
                         f.write(f"{fn['fine_id']}|{fn['username']}|{fn['borrow_id']}|{fn['amount']}|{fn['status']}|{fn['date_issued']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing fines data: {e}")
         
         # Lookup helpers
         
         def find_user(username: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for u in read_users():
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     return u
             return None
         
         
         def find_book(book_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for b in read_books():
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     return b
             return None
         
         
         def find_borrowing(borrow_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for b in read_borrowings():
                 if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                     return b
             return None
         
         
         def find_reservation(reservation_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for r in read_reservations():
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     return r
             return None
         
         
         def find_review(review_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for r in read_reviews():
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id:
                     return r
             return None
         
         
         def find_fine(fine_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for f in read_fines():
                 if f['fine_id'] == fine_id:
                     return f
             return None
         
         # Helper functions to generate unique IDs
         
         def next_borrow_id() -> int:
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             if not borrowings:
                 return 1
             return max(b['borrow_id'] for b in borrowings) + 1
         
         
         def next_reservation_id() -> int:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             if not reservations:
                 return 1
             return max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
         
         
         def next_review_id() -> int:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             if not reviews:
                 return 1
             return max(r['review_id'] for r in reviews) + 1
         
         
         def next_fine_id() -> int:
             fines = read_fines()
             if not fines:
                 return 1
             return max(f['fine_id'] for f in fines) + 1
         
         # Business Logic
         
         def calculate_due_date(from_date: datetime.date) -> datetime.date:
             return from_date + datetime.timedelta(days=14)
         
         
         def update_book_status(book_id: int, new_status: str) -> bool:
             books = read_books()
             updated = False
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     b['status'] = new_status
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_books(books)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_borrowing(borrow_id: int, new_status: str, return_date: Optional[str] = None, fine_amount: Optional[float] = None) -> bool:
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             updated = False
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                     b['status'] = new_status
                     if return_date is not None:
                         b['return_date'] = return_date
                     if fine_amount is not None:
                         b['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_reservation_status(reservation_id: int, new_status: str) -> bool:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             updated = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     r['status'] = new_status
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_review(review_id: int, rating: int, review_text: str, review_date: str) -> bool:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             updated = False
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id:
                     r['rating'] = rating
                     r['review_text'] = review_text
                     r['review_date'] = review_date
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_reviews(reviews)
             return updated
         
         
         def delete_review(review_id: int) -> bool:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             initial_len = len(reviews)
             reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['review_id'] != review_id]
             if len(reviews) < initial_len:
                 write_reviews(reviews)
                 return True
             return False
         
         
         def add_fine(username: str, borrow_id: int, amount: float) -> None:
             fines = read_fines()
             fine_id = next_fine_id()
             today = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             fines.append({
                 'fine_id': fine_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                 'amount': amount,
                 'status': 'Unpaid',
                 'date_issued': today
             })
             write_fines(fines)
         
         
         def calculate_fine(due_date_str: str, return_date_str: Optional[str]) -> float:
             try:
                 due_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(due_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                 if return_date_str:
                     return_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(return_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                 else:
                     return_date = datetime.date.today()
                 if return_date > due_date:
                     return float((return_date - due_date).days) * 1.0
                 return 0.0
             except Exception:
                 return 0.0
         
         # Logged user simulation
         LOGGED_USERNAME = 'john_reader'
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard_page():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             books = read_books()
             featured = sorted([b for b in books if b['status'] == 'Available'], key=lambda x: x['avg_rating'], reverse=True)[:3]
             featured_books = [{'book_id': b['book_id'], 'title': b['title']} for b in featured]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, featured_books=featured_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def catalog_page():
             books = read_books()
             books_list = [{'book_id': b['book_id'], 'title': b['title'], 'author': b['author'], 'status': b['status']} for b in books]
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             reviews = [r for r in read_reviews() if r['book_id'] == book_id]
             reviews_sorted = sorted(reviews, key=lambda r: r['review_date'], reverse=True)
             reviews_for_template = [{
                 'review_id': r['review_id'],
                 'username': r['username'],
                 'rating': r['rating'],
                 'review_text': r['review_text'],
                 'review_date': r['review_date']
             } for r in reviews_sorted]
         
             book_for_template = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'avg_rating': book['avg_rating']
             }
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book_for_template, reviews=reviews_for_template)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def borrow_confirmation(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if book['status'] != 'Available':
                     flash('This book is currently not available for borrowing.')
                     return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
                 return redirect(url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book_id))
         
             due_date = calculate_due_date(datetime.date.today()).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             book_simple = {'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']}
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book_simple, due_date=due_date)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_borrow(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Book not found.')
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Book is not available for borrowing.')
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             today_str = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date_str = calculate_due_date(datetime.date.today()).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             borrow_id = next_borrow_id()
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             borrowings.append({
                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': today_str,
                 'due_date': due_date_str,
                 'return_date': None,
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             })
             try:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
             except Exception as e:
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to save borrowing record.')
         
             if not update_book_status(book_id, 'Borrowed'):
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update book status.')
         
             return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=True, message=f'Borrowing confirmed for "{book["title"]}". Due date: {due_date_str}.')
         
         
         @app.route('/my_borrows')
         def my_borrowings():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             status_filter = request.args.get('status', 'All')
             filtered = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != username:
                     continue
                 if status_filter != 'All' and b['status'] != status_filter:
                     continue
                 book_title = next((book['title'] for book in books if book['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 filtered.append({
                     'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'due_date': b['due_date'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', username=username, borrows=filtered)
         
         
         @app.route('/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_borrow(borrow_id):
             borrowing = find_borrowing(borrow_id)
             if not borrowing:
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Borrowing record not found.')
             if borrowing['username'] != LOGGED_USERNAME:
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Unauthorized action.')
             if borrowing['status'] not in ('Active', 'Overdue'):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='This borrowing is no longer active.')
         
             today_str = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             fine_amt = calculate_fine(borrowing['due_date'], today_str)
         
             if not update_borrowing(borrow_id, 'Returned', today_str, fine_amt):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update borrowing.')
         
             if not update_book_status(borrowing['book_id'], 'Available'):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update book status.')
         
             if fine_amt > 0.0:
                 add_fine(LOGGED_USERNAME, borrow_id, fine_amt)
         
             msg = 'Book returned successfully.'
             if fine_amt > 0:
                 msg += f' Late return fine: ${fine_amt:.2f}. Please pay the fine.'
             return render_template('return_result.html', success=True, message=msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservations():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reservations = read_reservations()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reservations = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reservations.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                         'status': r['status']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', username=username, reservations=user_reservations)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservation = find_reservation(reservation_id)
             if not reservation:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Reservation not found.')
             if reservation['username'] != LOGGED_USERNAME:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Unauthorized action.')
             if reservation['status'] != 'Active':
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Reservation is not active.')
         
             if update_reservation_status(reservation_id, 'Cancelled'):
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=True, message='Reservation cancelled successfully.')
             else:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to cancel reservation.')
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_reviews():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reviews = read_reviews()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'review_date': r['review_date'],
                         'book_id': r['book_id']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', username=username, reviews=user_reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             existing_review = None
             for r in read_reviews():
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id and r['username'] == username:
                     existing_review = r
                     break
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rating = request.form.get('rating')
                 review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
                 if rating is None or not rating.isdigit() or int(rating) < 1 or int(rating) > 5:
                     flash('Invalid rating. Must be 1-5.')
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))
         
                 if not review_text:
                     flash('Review text cannot be empty.')
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))
         
                 review_date = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                 if existing_review:
                     if update_review(existing_review['review_id'], int(rating), review_text, review_date):
                         flash('Review updated successfully.')
                     else:
                         flash('Failed to update review.')
                     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
                 else:
                     new_review = {
                         'review_id': next_review_id(),
                         'username': username,
                         'book_id': book_id,
                         'rating': int(rating),
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': review_date
                     }
                     try:
                         reviews = read_reviews()
                         reviews.append(new_review)
                         write_reviews(reviews)
                         flash('Review added successfully.')
                     except:
                         flash('Failed to add review.')
                     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
         
             book_simple = {'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']}
             existing_review_simple = None
             if existing_review:
                 existing_review_simple = {
                     'review_id': existing_review['review_id'],
                     'rating': existing_review['rating'],
                     'review_text': existing_review['review_text']
                 }
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book_simple, existing_review=existing_review_simple)
         
         
         @app.route('/submit_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_review(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Book not found.')
         
             rating = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
             if rating is None or not rating.isdigit() or int(rating) < 1 or int(rating) > 5:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Invalid rating. Must be 1-5.')
             if not review_text:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Review text cannot be empty.')
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reviews = read_reviews()
             existing_review = None
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id and r['username'] == username:
                     existing_review = r
                     break
         
             review_date = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             if existing_review:
                 if update_review(existing_review['review_id'], int(rating), review_text, review_date):
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=True, message='Review updated successfully.')
                 else:
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update review.')
             else:
                 new_review = {
                     'review_id': next_review_id(),
                     'username': username,
                     'book_id': book_id,
                     'rating': int(rating),
                     'review_text': review_text,
                     'review_date': review_date
                 }
                 try:
                     reviews.append(new_review)
                     write_reviews(reviews)
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=True, message='Review added successfully.')
                 except:
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to add review.')
         
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             user = find_user(username)
             if not user:
                 flash('User profile not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             email = user['email']
             phone = user['phone']
             address = user['address']
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
             borrow_history = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     borrow_history.append({
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'return_date': b['return_date']
                     })
             return render_template('profile.html', username=username, email=email, phone=phone, address=address, borrow_history=borrow_history)
         
         
         @app.route('/update_profile', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             if not email:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='Email cannot be empty.')
         
             users = read_users()
             updated = False
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     u['email'] = email
                     u['phone'] = phone
                     u['address'] = address
                     updated = True
                     break
             if not updated:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='User not found.')
         
             try:
                 write_users(users)
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=True, message='Profile updated successfully.')
             except Exception as e:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update profile.')
         
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>')
         def payment_confirmation(fine_id):
             fine = find_fine(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine_amount=fine['amount'], fine_id=fine_id)
         
         
         @app.route('/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fine = find_fine(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Fine record not found.')
             if fine['status'] == 'Paid':
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Fine has already been paid.')
         
             if mark_fine_paid(fine_id):
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=True, message='Payment successful. Thank you.')
             else:
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Payment failed.')
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)

         from flask import Flask, render_template, redirect, url_for, request, flash
         import os
         import datetime
         from typing import List, Dict, Optional
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'replace_with_a_secure_key'
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         
         # File paths
         
         def users_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'users.txt')
         
         def books_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'books.txt')
         
         def borrowings_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'borrowings.txt')
         
         def reservations_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reservations.txt')
         
         def reviews_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'reviews.txt')
         
         def fines_filepath():
             return os.path.join(DATA_DIR, 'fines.txt')
         
         # Data loading functions
         
         def read_users() -> List[Dict]:
             users = []
             try:
                 with open(users_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 4:
                             continue
                         username, email, phone, address = parts
                         users.append({'username': username, 'email': email, 'phone': phone, 'address': address})
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading users data: {e}")
             return users
         
         
         def write_users(users: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(users_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for u in users:
                         f.write(f"{u['username']}|{u['email']}|{u['phone']}|{u['address']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing users data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_books() -> List[Dict]:
             books = []
             try:
                 with open(books_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 10:
                             continue
                         (book_id, title, author, isbn, genre, publisher, year, description, status, avg_rating) = parts
                         try:
                             books.append({
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'title': title,
                                 'author': author,
                                 'isbn': isbn,
                                 'genre': genre,
                                 'publisher': publisher,
                                 'year': int(year),
                                 'description': description,
                                 'status': status,
                                 'avg_rating': float(avg_rating)
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading books data: {e}")
             return books
         
         
         def write_books(books: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(books_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in books:
                         f.write(f"{b['book_id']}|{b['title']}|{b['author']}|{b['isbn']}|{b['genre']}|{b['publisher']}|{b['year']}|{b['description']}|{b['status']}|{b['avg_rating']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing books data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_borrowings() -> List[Dict]:
             borrowings = []
             try:
                 with open(borrowings_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 8:
                             continue
                         borrow_id, username, book_id, borrow_date, due_date, return_date, status, fine_amount = parts
                         try:
                             borrowings.append({
                                 'borrow_id': int(borrow_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'borrow_date': borrow_date,
                                 'due_date': due_date,
                                 'return_date': return_date if return_date else None,
                                 'status': status,
                                 'fine_amount': float(fine_amount)
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading borrowings data: {e}")
             return borrowings
         
         
         def write_borrowings(borrowings: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(borrowings_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for b in borrowings:
                         return_date = b['return_date'] if b['return_date'] else ''
                         f.write(f"{b['borrow_id']}|{b['username']}|{b['book_id']}|{b['borrow_date']}|{b['due_date']}|{return_date}|{b['status']}|{b['fine_amount']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing borrowings data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_reservations() -> List[Dict]:
             reservations = []
             try:
                 with open(reservations_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 5:
                             continue
                         reservation_id, username, book_id, reservation_date, status = parts
                         try:
                             reservations.append({
                                 'reservation_id': int(reservation_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'reservation_date': reservation_date,
                                 'status': status
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading reservations data: {e}")
             return reservations
         
         
         def write_reservations(reservations: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(reservations_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reservations:
                         f.write(f"{r['reservation_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['reservation_date']}|{r['status']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing reservations data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_reviews() -> List[Dict]:
             reviews = []
             try:
                 with open(reviews_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         review_id, username, book_id, rating, review_text, review_date = parts
                         try:
                             reviews.append({
                                 'review_id': int(review_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'book_id': int(book_id),
                                 'rating': int(rating),
                                 'review_text': review_text,
                                 'review_date': review_date
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading reviews data: {e}")
             return reviews
         
         
         def write_reviews(reviews: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(reviews_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for r in reviews:
                         f.write(f"{r['review_id']}|{r['username']}|{r['book_id']}|{r['rating']}|{r['review_text']}|{r['review_date']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing reviews data: {e}")
         
         
         def read_fines() -> List[Dict]:
             fines = []
             try:
                 with open(fines_filepath(), 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for line in f:
                         parts = line.strip().split('|')
                         if len(parts) != 6:
                             continue
                         fine_id, username, borrow_id, amount, status, date_issued = parts
                         try:
                             fines.append({
                                 'fine_id': int(fine_id),
                                 'username': username,
                                 'borrow_id': int(borrow_id),
                                 'amount': float(amount),
                                 'status': status,
                                 'date_issued': date_issued
                             })
                         except ValueError:
                             continue
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error reading fines data: {e}")
             return fines
         
         
         def write_fines(fines: List[Dict]) -> None:
             try:
                 with open(fines_filepath(), 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for fn in fines:
                         f.write(f"{fn['fine_id']}|{fn['username']}|{fn['borrow_id']}|{fn['amount']}|{fn['status']}|{fn['date_issued']}\n")
             except Exception as e:
                 flash(f"Error writing fines data: {e}")
         
         # Lookup helpers
         
         def find_user(username: str) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for u in read_users():
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     return u
             return None
         
         
         def find_book(book_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for b in read_books():
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     return b
             return None
         
         
         def find_borrowing(borrow_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for b in read_borrowings():
                 if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                     return b
             return None
         
         
         def find_reservation(reservation_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for r in read_reservations():
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     return r
             return None
         
         
         def find_review(review_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for r in read_reviews():
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id:
                     return r
             return None
         
         
         def find_fine(fine_id: int) -> Optional[Dict]:
             for f in read_fines():
                 if f['fine_id'] == fine_id:
                     return f
             return None
         
         # Helper functions to generate unique IDs
         
         def next_borrow_id() -> int:
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             if not borrowings:
                 return 1
             return max(b['borrow_id'] for b in borrowings) + 1
         
         
         def next_reservation_id() -> int:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             if not reservations:
                 return 1
             return max(r['reservation_id'] for r in reservations) + 1
         
         
         def next_review_id() -> int:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             if not reviews:
                 return 1
             return max(r['review_id'] for r in reviews) + 1
         
         
         def next_fine_id() -> int:
             fines = read_fines()
             if not fines:
                 return 1
             return max(f['fine_id'] for f in fines) + 1
         
         # Business Logic
         
         def calculate_due_date(from_date: datetime.date) -> datetime.date:
             return from_date + datetime.timedelta(days=14)
         
         
         def update_book_status(book_id: int, new_status: str) -> bool:
             books = read_books()
             updated = False
             for b in books:
                 if b['book_id'] == book_id:
                     b['status'] = new_status
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_books(books)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_borrowing(borrow_id: int, new_status: str, return_date: Optional[str] = None, fine_amount: Optional[float] = None) -> bool:
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             updated = False
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['borrow_id'] == borrow_id:
                     b['status'] = new_status
                     if return_date is not None:
                         b['return_date'] = return_date
                     if fine_amount is not None:
                         b['fine_amount'] = fine_amount
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_reservation_status(reservation_id: int, new_status: str) -> bool:
             reservations = read_reservations()
             updated = False
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['reservation_id'] == reservation_id:
                     r['status'] = new_status
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_reservations(reservations)
             return updated
         
         
         def update_review(review_id: int, rating: int, review_text: str, review_date: str) -> bool:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             updated = False
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['review_id'] == review_id:
                     r['rating'] = rating
                     r['review_text'] = review_text
                     r['review_date'] = review_date
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 write_reviews(reviews)
             return updated
         
         
         def delete_review(review_id: int) -> bool:
             reviews = read_reviews()
             initial_len = len(reviews)
             reviews = [r for r in reviews if r['review_id'] != review_id]
             if len(reviews) < initial_len:
                 write_reviews(reviews)
                 return True
             return False
         
         
         def add_fine(username: str, borrow_id: int, amount: float) -> None:
             fines = read_fines()
             fine_id = next_fine_id()
             today = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             fines.append({
                 'fine_id': fine_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                 'amount': amount,
                 'status': 'Unpaid',
                 'date_issued': today
             })
             write_fines(fines)
         
         
         def calculate_fine(due_date_str: str, return_date_str: Optional[str]) -> float:
             try:
                 due_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(due_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                 if return_date_str:
                     return_date = datetime.datetime.strptime(return_date_str, '%Y-%m-%d').date()
                 else:
                     return_date = datetime.date.today()
                 if return_date > due_date:
                     return float((return_date - due_date).days) * 1.0
                 return 0.0
             except Exception:
                 return 0.0
         
         # Logged user simulation
         LOGGED_USERNAME = 'john_reader'
         
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard_page():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             books = read_books()
             featured = sorted([b for b in books if b['status'] == 'Available'], key=lambda x: x['avg_rating'], reverse=True)[:3]
             featured_books = [{'book_id': b['book_id'], 'title': b['title']} for b in featured]
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, featured_books=featured_books)
         
         
         @app.route('/catalog')
         def catalog_page():
             books = read_books()
             books_list = [{'book_id': b['book_id'], 'title': b['title'], 'author': b['author'], 'status': b['status']} for b in books]
             return render_template('catalog.html', books=books_list)
         
         
         @app.route('/book/<int:book_id>')
         def book_details(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             reviews = [r for r in read_reviews() if r['book_id'] == book_id]
             reviews_sorted = sorted(reviews, key=lambda r: r['review_date'], reverse=True)
             reviews_for_template = [{
                 'review_id': r['review_id'],
                 'username': r['username'],
                 'rating': r['rating'],
                 'review_text': r['review_text'],
                 'review_date': r['review_date']
             } for r in reviews_sorted]
         
             book_for_template = {
                 'book_id': book['book_id'],
                 'title': book['title'],
                 'author': book['author'],
                 'status': book['status'],
                 'description': book['description'],
                 'avg_rating': book['avg_rating']
             }
             return render_template('book_details.html', book=book_for_template, reviews=reviews_for_template)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def borrow_confirmation(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 if book['status'] != 'Available':
                     flash('This book is currently not available for borrowing.')
                     return redirect(url_for('book_details', book_id=book_id))
                 return redirect(url_for('confirm_borrow', book_id=book_id))
         
             due_date = calculate_due_date(datetime.date.today()).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             book_simple = {'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']}
             return render_template('borrow_confirmation.html', book=book_simple, due_date=due_date)
         
         
         @app.route('/borrow/<int:book_id>/confirm', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_borrow(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Book not found.')
             if book['status'] != 'Available':
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Book is not available for borrowing.')
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             today_str = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             due_date_str = calculate_due_date(datetime.date.today()).strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             borrow_id = next_borrow_id()
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             borrowings.append({
                 'borrow_id': borrow_id,
                 'username': username,
                 'book_id': book_id,
                 'borrow_date': today_str,
                 'due_date': due_date_str,
                 'return_date': None,
                 'status': 'Active',
                 'fine_amount': 0.0
             })
             try:
                 write_borrowings(borrowings)
             except Exception as e:
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to save borrowing record.')
         
             if not update_book_status(book_id, 'Borrowed'):
                 return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update book status.')
         
             return render_template('borrow_result.html', success=True, message=f'Borrowing confirmed for "{book["title"]}". Due date: {due_date_str}.')
         
         
         @app.route('/my_borrows')
         def my_borrowings():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
         
             status_filter = request.args.get('status', 'All')
             filtered = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] != username:
                     continue
                 if status_filter != 'All' and b['status'] != status_filter:
                     continue
                 book_title = next((book['title'] for book in books if book['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                 filtered.append({
                     'borrow_id': b['borrow_id'],
                     'book_title': book_title,
                     'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                     'due_date': b['due_date'],
                     'status': b['status']
                 })
         
             return render_template('my_borrows.html', username=username, borrows=filtered)
         
         
         @app.route('/return_borrow/<int:borrow_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def return_borrow(borrow_id):
             borrowing = find_borrowing(borrow_id)
             if not borrowing:
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Borrowing record not found.')
             if borrowing['username'] != LOGGED_USERNAME:
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Unauthorized action.')
             if borrowing['status'] not in ('Active', 'Overdue'):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='This borrowing is no longer active.')
         
             today_str = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
             fine_amt = calculate_fine(borrowing['due_date'], today_str)
         
             if not update_borrowing(borrow_id, 'Returned', today_str, fine_amt):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update borrowing.')
         
             if not update_book_status(borrowing['book_id'], 'Available'):
                 return render_template('return_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update book status.')
         
             if fine_amt > 0.0:
                 add_fine(LOGGED_USERNAME, borrow_id, fine_amt)
         
             msg = 'Book returned successfully.'
             if fine_amt > 0:
                 msg += f' Late return fine: ${fine_amt:.2f}. Please pay the fine.'
             return render_template('return_result.html', success=True, message=msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reservations')
         def my_reservations():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reservations = read_reservations()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reservations = []
             for r in reservations:
                 if r['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reservations.append({
                         'reservation_id': r['reservation_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'reservation_date': r['reservation_date'],
                         'status': r['status']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reservations.html', username=username, reservations=user_reservations)
         
         
         @app.route('/cancel_reservation/<int:reservation_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def cancel_reservation(reservation_id):
             reservation = find_reservation(reservation_id)
             if not reservation:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Reservation not found.')
             if reservation['username'] != LOGGED_USERNAME:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Unauthorized action.')
             if reservation['status'] != 'Active':
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Reservation is not active.')
         
             if update_reservation_status(reservation_id, 'Cancelled'):
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=True, message='Reservation cancelled successfully.')
             else:
                 return render_template('cancel_reservation_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to cancel reservation.')
         
         
         @app.route('/my_reviews')
         def my_reviews():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reviews = read_reviews()
             books = read_books()
         
             user_reviews = []
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((b['title'] for b in books if b['book_id'] == r['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     user_reviews.append({
                         'review_id': r['review_id'],
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'rating': r['rating'],
                         'review_text': r['review_text'],
                         'review_date': r['review_date'],
                         'book_id': r['book_id']
                     })
             return render_template('my_reviews.html', username=username, reviews=user_reviews)
         
         
         @app.route('/write_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def write_review(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 flash('Book not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('catalog_page'))
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             existing_review = None
             for r in read_reviews():
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id and r['username'] == username:
                     existing_review = r
                     break
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 rating = request.form.get('rating')
                 review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
                 if rating is None or not rating.isdigit() or int(rating) < 1 or int(rating) > 5:
                     flash('Invalid rating. Must be 1-5.')
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))
         
                 if not review_text:
                     flash('Review text cannot be empty.')
                     return redirect(url_for('write_review', book_id=book_id))
         
                 review_date = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
                 if existing_review:
                     if update_review(existing_review['review_id'], int(rating), review_text, review_date):
                         flash('Review updated successfully.')
                     else:
                         flash('Failed to update review.')
                     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
                 else:
                     new_review = {
                         'review_id': next_review_id(),
                         'username': username,
                         'book_id': book_id,
                         'rating': int(rating),
                         'review_text': review_text,
                         'review_date': review_date
                     }
                     try:
                         reviews = read_reviews()
                         reviews.append(new_review)
                         write_reviews(reviews)
                         flash('Review added successfully.')
                     except:
                         flash('Failed to add review.')
                     return redirect(url_for('my_reviews'))
         
             book_simple = {'book_id': book['book_id'], 'title': book['title'], 'author': book['author']}
             existing_review_simple = None
             if existing_review:
                 existing_review_simple = {
                     'review_id': existing_review['review_id'],
                     'rating': existing_review['rating'],
                     'review_text': existing_review['review_text']
                 }
             return render_template('write_review.html', book=book_simple, existing_review=existing_review_simple)
         
         
         @app.route('/submit_review/<int:book_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def submit_review(book_id):
             book = find_book(book_id)
             if not book:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Book not found.')
         
             rating = request.form.get('rating')
             review_text = request.form.get('review_text', '').strip()
         
             if rating is None or not rating.isdigit() or int(rating) < 1 or int(rating) > 5:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Invalid rating. Must be 1-5.')
             if not review_text:
                 return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Review text cannot be empty.')
         
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             reviews = read_reviews()
             existing_review = None
             for r in reviews:
                 if r['book_id'] == book_id and r['username'] == username:
                     existing_review = r
                     break
         
             review_date = datetime.date.today().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
         
             if existing_review:
                 if update_review(existing_review['review_id'], int(rating), review_text, review_date):
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=True, message='Review updated successfully.')
                 else:
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update review.')
             else:
                 new_review = {
                     'review_id': next_review_id(),
                     'username': username,
                     'book_id': book_id,
                     'rating': int(rating),
                     'review_text': review_text,
                     'review_date': review_date
                 }
                 try:
                     reviews.append(new_review)
                     write_reviews(reviews)
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=True, message='Review added successfully.')
                 except:
                     return render_template('review_submit_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to add review.')
         
         
         @app.route('/profile')
         def user_profile():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             user = find_user(username)
             if not user:
                 flash('User profile not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('dashboard_page'))
         
             email = user['email']
             phone = user['phone']
             address = user['address']
         
             borrowings = read_borrowings()
             books = read_books()
             borrow_history = []
             for b in borrowings:
                 if b['username'] == username:
                     book_title = next((bk['title'] for bk in books if bk['book_id'] == b['book_id']), 'Unknown')
                     borrow_history.append({
                         'book_title': book_title,
                         'borrow_date': b['borrow_date'],
                         'return_date': b['return_date']
                     })
             return render_template('profile.html', username=username, email=email, phone=phone, address=address, borrow_history=borrow_history)
         
         
         @app.route('/update_profile', methods=['POST'])
         def update_profile():
             username = LOGGED_USERNAME
             email = request.form.get('email', '').strip()
             phone = request.form.get('phone', '').strip()
             address = request.form.get('address', '').strip()
         
             if not email:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='Email cannot be empty.')
         
             users = read_users()
             updated = False
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     u['email'] = email
                     u['phone'] = phone
                     u['address'] = address
                     updated = True
                     break
             if not updated:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='User not found.')
         
             try:
                 write_users(users)
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=True, message='Profile updated successfully.')
             except Exception as e:
                 return render_template('profile_update_result.html', success=False, message='Failed to update profile.')
         
         
         @app.route('/payment/<int:fine_id>')
         def payment_confirmation(fine_id):
             fine = find_fine(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 flash('Fine record not found.')
                 return redirect(url_for('user_profile'))
             return render_template('payment_confirmation.html', fine_amount=fine['amount'], fine_id=fine_id)
         
         
         @app.route('/confirm_payment/<int:fine_id>', methods=['POST'])
         def confirm_payment(fine_id):
             fine = find_fine(fine_id)
             if not fine:
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Fine record not found.')
             if fine['status'] == 'Paid':
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Fine has already been paid.')
         
             if mark_fine_paid(fine_id):
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=True, message='Payment successful. Thank you.')
             else:
                 return render_template('payment_result.html', success=False, message='Payment failed.')
         
         
         if __name__ == '__main__':
             app.run(debug=True)
